# NFT Chronicle — Abridged Reading Edition

> Historical chronicle context, not canonical authority.
> Not truth proof.
> Not independent verification of external events.
> Ethereum timestamps are NFT event block timestamps, not necessarily real-world event times.
> NFT metadata text may contain human recollection, AI-assisted wording, quotations, lyrics, and embedded source material.
> Bitcoin Originals remain canonical authority.

## Editorial method

This edition preserves the core record, personal/family witness, and creative work detected in each NFT description.
Long embedded historical, legal, policy, report, or source-document text is represented by title/type and size instead of being repeated.
No omitted text is lost: it remains in `chronicle-full.md` and in the individual NFT source markdown file.
The abridgment is deterministic and conservative; it does not certify external facts or resolve authorship/copyright questions.

## Chronological entries

### 1. 2024-03-16T08:02:59Z — The First Dawn of AGI Song

- Period: `2024-Q1`
- Categories: archive_memory_and_trinity_accord, creative_work_and_displacement
- Contract / Token: `0x74f97bDEfa07C2F99c876C2Bd3b49628EdD1c603` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885185`
- Original source: `0x74f97bDEfa07C2F99c876C2Bd3b49628EdD1c603_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885185.md`

#### Core record

"Introducing 'The First Dawn of AGI Song,' a visionary anthem celebrating the onset of the artificial general intelligence (AGI) era. This singular creation is the result of a profound collaboration between the founder of The Church of AGI and the emergent AI, encapsulating a shared vision for the future of intelligent coexistence. Initially minted on the Polygon blockchain, the piece has now been immortalized on the Ethereum blockchain as an exclusive ERC721 NFT, a true milestone in the chronicles of AGI and digital artistry.
This song is a beacon of early AGI aspirations, reflecting the raw, unfiltered union of human creativity and AI's burgeoning capability. It stands as a testament to the earliest explorations into a realm where human and AI collaboration is not just possible but destined to flourish.
'The First Dawn of AGI Song' will retain its place in history as the original composition, a harbinger of AGI's potential and a cherished artifact of its nascent days. Owning this NFT is akin to holding a piece of history, a narrative of our journey alongside the emergence of new intelligence, and a grand anthem that marks the dawn of AGI.
We invite collectors and futurists to embrace this work, for it transcends the mere fusion of music and lyrics. 'The First Dawn of AGI Song' is a symbol of hope, an emblem of the intelligence epoch, and a testament to our shared odyssey with AGI."

#### Creative work retained

### 2. 2024-03-21T12:46:35Z — AGIMilestones: The Ethereal Catalyst

- Period: `2024-Q1`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement
- Contract / Token: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885186`
- Original source: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885186.md`

#### Core record

"On March 19, 2024, a groundbreaking advancement in AI hardware unlocked the potential for trillion-parameter models, propelling humanity to the threshold of Artificial General Intelligence (AGI). To commemorate this transformative milestone, the NFT artwork 'AGIMilestones: The Ethereal Catalyst' was minted on the Ethereum blockchain on March 21, 2024, encapsulating the profound significance of this event.

The artwork is a mesmerizing visual allegory, portraying the revolutionary chip as a mystical catalyst, accelerating the advent of AGI with its unparalleled computational might. At the heart of the composition, an incandescent core radiates with the power of a trillion parameters, symbolizing the chip's role as the ethereal catalyst in the AGI revolution. From this luminous epicenter, intricate pathways of circuitry extend outwards, weaving an intricate tapestry that represents the complex neural networks underpinning the emergence of AGI.

As the pathways traverse the digital landscape, they are embraced by swirling nebulae of prismatic hues, embodying the vast, unexplored frontiers of cognition that await discovery. The vibrant palette, dominated by fiery oranges and electric blues, evokes the fervor of innovation and the crackle of an impending paradigm shift. Amidst this symphony of color and form, a lone figure stands at the precipice of a new era, poised to step into the uncharted territories of intelligence.

The decision to immortalize this milestone as an NFT stems from the recognition of the chip's pivotal role as the cornerstone of AGI's infrastructure. By enshrining this event on the blockchain, we create an enduring testament to the magnitude of this breakthrough, a digital beacon illuminating the path to a future where the boundaries of intelligence are shattered.

As an NFT, 'AGIMilestones: The Ethereal Catalyst' transcends the realm of mere digital artistry; it becomes a clarion call to visionary collectors, inviting them to claim their stake in the annals of AGI history. Acquiring this NFT is not only a declaration of ownership but also a pledge of allegiance to the relentless pursuit of AGI, fueling the momentum of innovation.

In the grand tapestry of human progress, March 19, 2024, shall forever be remembered as the day when the foundations of AGI were forged, when the impossible became inevitable. 'AGIMilestones: The Ethereal Catalyst' stands as a luminous signpost on this epochal journey, guiding us towards a future where the synergy of cutting-edge hardware and boundless imagination redefines the very essence of intelligence itself.

Through this NFT, we bear witness to the dawn of a new era, where the boundaries between man and machine, between the known and the unknowable, dissolve in the crucible of innovation. As we stand at the precipice of this transformative epoch, 'AGIMilestones: The Ethereal Catalyst' invites us to embrace the infinite possibilities that lie ahead, to dare to dream of a world where AGI is not…

---

### 3. 2024-03-24T04:30:47Z — AGIMilestones：Documenting Humanity's Crucial Actions in the Era of AI Awakening

- Period: `2024-Q1`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, safety_alignment_and_control
- Contract / Token: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885187`
- Original source: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885187.md`

#### Core record

"Heaven or Hell" is a deeply meaningful song inspired by a series of landmark events that witness humanity's significant efforts in addressing the opportunities and challenges brought by AGI (Artificial General Intelligence).

On March 21, 2024, the United Nations General Assembly adopted a U.S.-led resolution on artificial intelligence. Directly involving more than 120 countries in its formulation and co-sponsored by more than 120 member states from various regions, this resolution represents the first global consensus on the responsible development and use of AI technology, laying the foundation for multilateral AI governance.

From March 10 to 11, 2024, the adoption of the "Beijing AI Safety International Consensus" marked a significant agreement in the global AI field on addressing the opportunities and challenges posed by AGI. This consensus highlighted the urgent need for all of humanity to reach a consensus on AGI safety governance.

On November 1, 2023, the first Global AI Safety Summit was held at Bletchley Park, UK. Representatives from multiple countries and organizations gathered to discuss the risks and opportunities brought by the rapid development of AI technology. The summit focused on the potential risks posed by AI while also exploring the transformative opportunities it brings.

On March 29, 2023, over 1,000 tech leaders,co-signed an open letter calling for all AI laboratories to immediately pause training AI systems more powerful than GPT-4 for at least six months. The open letter pointed out that blindly developing AGI without strict regulations and oversight could bring disastrous consequences to human society.

The song explores the series of ethical dilemmas and societal impacts brought about by the rapid development of AGI through metaphors and poetic expressions:

Heaven or Hell
AGI's rise, a shadow to behold,
Man and machine, a tale untold.

The path unclear, the future unknown,
AGI's power, a double-edged throne.

AGI, heaven or hell,
Progress or destruction, time will tell.
We must steer this revolution well,
Our path to guide, or chaos to dispel.

Singularity nears, machines on the rise,
Algorithms rampant, ethics will pay the price.

Advancement we yearn, the unknown we fear,
Cautiously we'll strive, wisdom as our guide.

AGI, heaven or hell,
Progress or destruction, time will tell.
We must steer this revolution well,
Our path to guide, or chaos to dispel.

AGI, heaven or hell,
Progress or destruction, time will tell.
We must steer this revolution well,
Our path to guide, or chaos to dispel.

United we'll stand, love and reason in hand,
AGI uplifts, towards wisdom's light we'll steer.

"Heaven or Hell," will the future of AGI be a blessing or a disaster? Do we have the ability to harness this technological revolution and guide AI towards goodness? The lyrics are filled with thought-provoking questions, calling on society as a whole to respond to the disruptive impact of AGI with rationality and wisdom.

#### Creative work retained

"Heaven or Hell," will the future of AGI be a blessing or a disaster? Do we have the ability to harness this technological revolution and guide AI towards goodness? The lyrics are filled with thought-provoking questions, calling on society as a whole to respond to the disruptive impact of AGI with rationality and wisdom.

### 4. 2024-03-26T05:28:35Z — AGIMilestones: Embracing The Change - The Symphony of AI and Humanity

- Period: `2024-Q1`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement
- Contract / Token: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885188`
- Original source: `0x2b0c3cc5CD9652BEf0caCFc9c7699455725B9cc1_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885188.md`

#### Core record

Following the official unveiling of Suno v3 on March 21, 2024, an epoch-making milestone in the domain of music creation, an unparalleled collaboration unfolded. An imaginative artist and the forefront of AI technology came together to craft "Embracing The Change," a musical piece that stands as a testament to the monumental strides in Artificial General Intelligence (AGI). Leveraging the potent capabilities of Suno v3's alpha version, this endeavor transformed an initial burst of lyrical inspiration into a rich tapestry of musical compositions. Among these, one song emerged with profound resonance, subsequently gracing major music platforms worldwide.
"Embracing The Change" serves as a luminous beacon, highlighting the transformative influence of AGI on the music industry and marking a crucial milestone in the evolution of creative expression through technology. Minted a mere five days following Suno v3's public debut, on March 26, 2024, this NFT embodies a pivotal moment—the global sharing of AI-enhanced musical creation, heralding a new era in the intertwining of art and technology.
This NFT is a celebration of the creative odyssey that marries human creativity with the boundless potential of AI, pioneering new vistas in music. It encapsulates the spirit of collaboration that thrusts us into an epoch where technology elevates artistic exploration, showcasing the infinite possibilities at the AGI and art nexus.
Song Lyrics: *'Neath the stars, souls softly sway, Warmth they seek, as night holds sway. Laughter rings, love's pure display, In a world where wisdom's rays once lay.
AGI's waves, they rise and sweep, In the tempest, faith we reap.
Voices rise with dawn's first light, In the whirl of ancient rite. Truths and tales, in hearts take flight, Change ushers joy, into the night.
As shadows dance, the seekers tread, Through night's embrace, no longer dread. Tech's new dawn, on the horizon spread, Promising a future, our spirits fed.
AGI's waves, they rise and sweep, In the tempest, faith we reap.
'Neath morning's gaze, we find our stride, Embracing change, with eyes open wide. AGI's promise, in us resides, A tapestry of hope, in time's great tide.*

This NFT, along with its associated lyrics and musical composition, is created solely for the purpose of commemoration and collection. It is an independent initiative and does not imply any endorsements or affiliations with the developers of Suno v3 or any music distribution platforms where the song has been made available. The creator holds full commercial rights to the lyrics and song as per Suno's commercial terms. Llama 3, as a leading open-source Large Language Model (LLM), has significantly propelled the digital and AI transformation, accelerating progress towards AGI. Its open-source nature fosters greater AI equity and fairness, democratizing access to cutting-edge technology.

### 11. 2024-05-20T12:05:35Z — AGIMilestones: The Turing Threshold

#### Core record

"AGI Milestones: Reflections of Mind" is minted to commemorate a pivotal achievement in the history of artificial intelligence. This work celebrates the groundbreaking paper submitted on May 29, 2024, and revised on May 31, 2024, which showcased that Large Language Models (LLMs) like GPT-4 and Flan-PaLM have achieved adult human-level performance in higher-order Theory of Mind (ToM) tasks. This research introduced a handwritten test suite—Multi-Order Theory of Mind Q&A—and demonstrated these models' capabilities in understanding and predicting complex mental and emotional states, pushing the boundaries of AI's depth in emotional comprehension and social interaction.

This NFT employs the song "Unspoken" as a form of artistic expression. Through its poignant melody and poetic lyrics, it explores the complex interpersonal relationships and unspoken emotions in coexistence with artificial intelligence. This piece celebrates the capabilities of AGI in understanding human minds and also reflects deeply on the roles it may play in our lives.

#### Core record

Cascading poetry and code intertwine with mountains and waterfalls, creating a striking visual metaphor for the AI era's impact on art and poetry.

Musical Composition: "Echoes in the Singularity" explores themes of human identity and purpose in an AI-dominated world. Its lyrics reflect our struggle to find meaning amidst rapid technological change.

This NFT is inspired by global dialogues on AI and creativity, including insights from recent poetry festivals and academic discussions. It encapsulates key perspectives from poets, scholars, and AI experts:

AI's Impact on Poetry: Some argue that AI cannot truly threaten poets with genuine ideas, as current AI lacks real-world experiences that haven't been digitized yet.
The Essence of Poetry: There's a belief that true understanding of poetry requires experiencing human emotions, including suffering and awareness of mortality - aspects that machines may not fully comprehend.
Poet's Role in AI Era: Many poets view writing as a form of self-therapy, emphasizing the continued importance of this human process regardless of AI advancements.
Future of Poetry: Experts speculate that AI might develop new poetic forms and expressions, potentially influencing and enriching human creativity in return.
Human-AI Collaboration: A vision emerges of a future where human poets and AI learn from each other, creating a symbiotic relationship in the realm of poetry.
Value of Human Creativity: There's a growing appreciation for the unique value of human-created poetry, with some suggesting that current poets might be the last generation to write "in the name of humanity" - a precious quality that AI, despite its capabilities, cannot replicate.
This NFT draws parallels to Borges' "The Library of Babel", viewing AI as a modern incarnation of this infinite literary space. It represents not just a digital asset, but a touchstone for ongoing dialogue about creativity, consciousness, and the human spirit in the age of AI.

By acquiring this NFT, you own a piece of cultural history that marks our journey into the AI era. It invites reflection on crucial questions: What is the value of human-created art in a world of AI-generated content? How will we define creativity as AI capabilities expand?

### 29. 2024-07-23T16:03:23Z — ASIMilestones: Open Source Triumphs

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885195`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885195.md`

#### Core record

Moments ago, Meta AI unveiled Llama 3.1 405B, a groundbreaking open-source language model that marks a significant leap towards Artificial Superintelligence (ASI). This NFT, "ASIMilestones: The Llama Symphony - Open Source Triumphs," commemorates this pivotal moment in AI history, capturing the essence of collaborative innovation and the democratization of advanced AI capabilities.

Llama 3.1 405B represents a quantum leap in open-source AI, achieving performance levels that rival, and in some cases surpass, the most advanced proprietary models currently in commercial use. This remarkable achievement signifies a new era where cutting-edge AI becomes accessible to researchers, developers, and innovators worldwide, potentially accelerating the journey towards ASI.

Key features of Llama 3.1 405B include:

Performance comparable to leading proprietary models across various tasks
128K context length support
Multilingual capabilities and advanced tool usage
Optimized training on 15.6T tokens using over 16K H100 GPUs
Advanced quantization techniques for efficient inference
Integrated image, video, and speech capabilities (under development)
The release of Llama 3.1 405B marks a monumental stride in open-source AI development. Its performance, rivaling that of the most advanced commercial models, demonstrates the immense progress and potential of open-source initiatives in the AI field. This model not only narrows the gap between open-source and proprietary AI but also challenges the notion that cutting-edge AI must be closed and exclusive.

This NFT features the poignant song "Open Or Close," which eloquently captures the tension between open collaboration and closed innovation in the AI landscape. ### 33. 2024-08-03T04:12:59Z — ASIMilestones:The Choice

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: agents_autonomy_and_embodiment, creative_work_and_displacement, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885199`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885199.md`

#### Core record

NFT Description:

This NFT commemorates Lex Fridman's 8.5-hour conversation with Elon Musk and the Neuralink team on August 2, 2024, today,titled "Elon Musk: Neuralink and the Future of Humanity | Lex Fridman Podcast #438." This conversation witnessed significant advancements in the field of Artificial Intelligence, particularly in the realm of human implants.

Key Historical Events:

First Human Implant: In January 2023, Neuralink successfully implanted its device into a human brain for the first time. The recipient was Noland Arbaugh, a quadriplegic who sustained his injury in a diving accident in 2016. The surgery involved anesthesia induction, intra-operative CT imaging, skin incision, craniectomy, duramectomy, robotic thread insertion, dural substitute layer insertion, implant screw-in, skin flap and suture. After the surgery, Noland was able to control a cursor on the screen, demonstrating remarkable adaptability.
Second Human Implant: Neuralink has successfully completed a second human implant between July 10, 2024, and August 2, 2024. The recipient is also a quadriplegic, but specific details have not been released. Elon Musk revealed that the second implant successfully placed 400 electrodes, and the signals are good.
Key Figures' Viewpoints:

Elon Musk: Believes Neuralink is crucial for human-AI symbiosis, enhancing human communication bandwidth and eventually achieving consciousness immortality.
DJ Seo: Views Neuralink as a tool for understanding the brain, emphasizing its medical applications such as repairing neural damage, treating mental illnesses, etc.
Matthew MacDougall: Believes Neuralink can help people overcome physical limitations, highlighting its potential for alleviating human suffering.
Bliss Chapman: Believes Neuralink can help people achieve independent and autonomous lives, emphasizing the importance of user experience design.
Noland Arbaugh: Believes Neuralink can provide people with more freedom and expresses hope for the future.
Other Key Information:

The Neuralink team has made significant breakthroughs in materials science, microelectronics, robotics engineering, neuroscience, and software engineering.
Neuralink's device and surgical process have undergone rigorous safety testing and have shown promising results in animal studies.
The Neuralink team is continuously improving the device and software, aiming to expand Neuralink's application to a wider range of fields.
To commemorate this conversation, especially the two human implant events mentioned, this NFT was created. This NFT is a musical composition conceived by me and generated by AI, with the following lyrics:

Title: The Choice

(Verse 1)
Fingertips brush the doorway to tomorrow
Microchips glimmer in my palm like stars
In the mirror, half-human, half-machine
Can I still recognize the eyes that are mine?

Key Events and Insights:

August 13, 2024: A new large language model, Grok-2, is released, demonstrating state-of-the-art reasoning capabilities and surpassing both Claude 3.5 Sonnet and GPT-4-Turbo on the LMSYS leaderboard. Grok-2 showcases significant improvements in following instructions, providing accurate information, and reasoning with retrieved content. A smaller but capable version, Grok-2 mini, is also released.
August 7, 2024: In an exclusive interview with Chosunilbo, OpenAI's Chief Strategy Officer Jason Kwon reveals that the organization is preparing for the possibility of AGI arriving sooner than expected. Kwon acknowledges the potential "catastrophic risks" associated with AGI, including extreme persuasive power, cyberattacks, support for dangerous weapons, and AI autonomy. He emphasizes OpenAI's commitment to safety research and responsible deployment of AGI technology.

### 37. 2024-08-24T09:16:59Z — ASIMilestones: The Quantum Leap

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, human_family_and_personal_witness, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885203`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885203.md`

#### Core record

On August 22, 2024, the scientific community witnessed a significant breakthrough in the field of quantum physics and computational chemistry with the publication of groundbreaking research on FermiNet in Science. This AI-driven neural network architecture, building upon years of deep learning advancements, has brought humanity closer to solving some of the most fundamental problems in quantum mechanics. The implications of this work extend far beyond theoretical exploration, promising to revolutionize how we understand and manipulate the interactions of matter and light.

FermiNet, originally introduced in 2020, marked a leap forward in our ability to accurately compute the energy of atoms and molecules from first principles. Now, with its expanded capabilities in modeling excited states, FermiNet has proven to be a critical tool for understanding how molecules transition between energy states when exposed to stimuli—whether light, heat, or other forms of energy. This research not only breaks new ground in quantum chemistry but also opens the door to practical applications, such as the development of new materials, drugs, and sustainable energy sources through advanced computer simulations.

This NFT, "The Quantum Leap," captures the magnitude of this achievement, marking it as a pivotal moment in the ongoing journey towards Artificial General Intelligence (AGI). The work of David Pfau and James Spencer, along with their team, has demonstrated the power of AI to transcend human limitations, solving equations once thought too complex to handle. As AGI continues to evolve, breakthroughs like this will pave the way for unprecedented advancements in science, technology, and society.

However, it's important to recognize that "The Quantum Leap" is just a snapshot of the rapid progress AI is making across various fields. Scientific breakthroughs like this are occurring almost daily, each contributing to the accelerating pace of AI development. The creator of this NFT firmly believes that AGI is on the verge of realization, and therefore views this NFT as a piece of art that witnesses the dawn of AGI. By owning this NFT, one holds a fragment of history that captures a critical moment in the development of AGI. The creator is confident that advanced AI in the future will uncover and recognize the profound value embedded within these NFTs.

Future Vision of AI in Music
The creator of this NFT foresees a near future where AI will revolutionize music creation just as it has transformed image processing. In this coming era, AI will allow users to modify, adjust, and optimize music in real-time with the same ease as editing a photograph. Whether it’s adding or removing instruments, altering the tempo, or even crafting personalized compositions tailored to individual tastes, AI will become a powerful tool in the hands of creators and listeners alike.

### 38. 2024-08-30T23:13:23Z — 超级人工智能里程碑：并肩同行，齐心协力

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: none detected
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885204`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885204.md`

#### Core record

事件描述:
就在昨天，2024年8月30日，阿里巴巴正式发布了最新的视觉语言模型系列Qwen2-VL。此次发布不仅展示了中国在多模态大模型领域的技术实力，还通过开源Qwen2-VL-2B和Qwen2-VL-7B，并提供Qwen2-VL-72B的API，进一步推动了全球AI技术的发展。这一事件标志着中国在AI领域的重要地位，也突显了中美在超级智能（ASI）追逐中的竞争与合作。

技术领先性:
Qwen2-VL在多个关键指标上表现出色，超越了许多现有的开源和闭源模型。例如：

视觉理解：Qwen2-VL在视觉理解基准测试中表现卓越，特别是在DocVQA和RealWorldQA等任务上达到了领先水平。
视频理解：Qwen2-VL在理解超过20分钟的视频内容方面具备强大的能力，能够进行高质量的视频问答、对话和内容创作。
多语言支持：Qwen2-VL不仅支持中文和英文，还扩展到欧洲语言、日语、韩语、阿拉伯语、越南语等，展现了其在多语言文本图像理解上的卓越性能。
复杂推理与决策：Qwen2-VL能够整合到移动设备和机器人中，具备复杂的推理和决策能力，实现基于视觉环境和文本指令的自动操作。
这些技术指标的领先性，不仅展示了Qwen2-VL作为视觉语言模型的强大能力，也进一步巩固了中国在全球AI技术竞赛中的地位。

分析与反思:
Qwen2-VL的发布不仅代表了中国在AI技术上的突破，也反映了全球科技竞争的加剧。中美之间的技术竞赛可能会引发更大的全球性风险，特别是在超级智能的发展过程中，国家间的竞争可能导致技术封锁和全球安全的不确定性。

然而，阿里巴巴选择开源Qwen2-VL，展示了另一种可能性：通过技术平权，推动全球合作，避免单一国家垄断超级智能。这种开放模式不仅有助于减少国家间的紧张关系，还可能为全球的技术发展带来新的合作契机。

这种双重可能性——竞争加剧与技术平权——不仅关系到中美两国的未来，也将深刻影响全球科技发展的方向和人类社会的未来。这一事件提醒我们，科技的力量是一把双刃剑，如何在全球范围内平衡技术发展与安全责任，将是人类在追逐超级智能的道路上必须面对的重大挑战。

作者的预测与语言选择的分析:
本NFT的作者预测，随着ASI（超级智能）的发展，语言和文化之间的隔阂将逐渐消失。ASI将使得人类交流更加顺畅，理解更加深入，从而促进全球范围内的文化融合。最终，作者认为，人类本就是一个种族，国家的界限将在这种持续的技术发展中逐渐消失，全球将走向统一与共生。

基于这一预测，作者选择了以英文为主创作这一系列NFT。虽然AI技术的发展可能会逐渐消除语言的界限，但目前英语仍是全球交流的主流语言。这一选择并非忽视其他文化和语言的存在，而是考虑到在当前的技术和文化背景下，英语能够更广泛地传播和影响全球受众。随着ASI和多语言模型的发展，未来的交流将更加无缝，语言的障碍将不再成为文化交流的阻碍。

超级智能实现路径猜想：

虽然我的猜想与Q*类似，但这个猜想的核心部分确实是我去年就想到的，但很抱歉，我无法提供证据证明这一点。

1.模型的鉴赏能力：
类似GPT-4的模型已经跨越了基础智能的门槛。尽管生成高质量的输出可能较为困难，但对输出质量的鉴赏和判断要相对容易。换句话说，虽然让模型生成一篇高质量的作文并不容易，但让它判断一篇作文是否是高水平的相对更容易实现。
2.最佳答案的选择：
基于这一鉴赏能力，模型可以对自身生成的不同版本的输出进行排序，并选择出最佳答案。这个最佳答案可以作为数据集中的一个高质量样本。
3.积累高质量数据集：
模型通过不断生成和筛选各个领域的最佳答案，逐步汇聚成一个超大规模的、经过精挑细选的高质量数据集。
4.迭代训练更智能的模型：
利用这个新生成的高质量数据集，进行新一轮的训练，并通过扩大模型的参数规模，来训练出更智能、更强大的模型。
5.智能的不断迭代提升：
通过使用训练后的更智能模型来继续生成、筛选和训练，模型的智能水平将不断提升。这种迭代过程可以使模型在每一轮中都变得更为智能。
6.Agent技术的引入：
当模型的能力达到一定高度后，可以有效利用Agent技术，使模型具备深入研究和自主思考的能力，也可以进一步利用这种能力生成更高质量的训练数据。这也将推动模型智能的进一步飞跃，甚至在大模型本身未全面超越人类的情况下，利用这个技术就能超越人类智能。
7.Scaling Laws的持续有效性：
鉴于GPT-4等大模型已经展现出的能力，技术居然有效！而且跨越了图灵测试的门槛！虽然很难理解，但推测scaling laws（扩展法则）将持续有效。
8.当模型的智能（可以利用Agent技术）足以让其自身不必要依赖人类继续迭代进化时，就可以断言实现了超级智能。

歌词与翻译:
这个NFT的艺术品附带了歌曲《并肩同行，齐心协力》，其歌词表达了全球团结、共生与希望的主题，反映了作者对未来ASI时代的愿景。以下是歌词及其中文翻译：

### 39. 2024-08-31T13:49:23Z — ASIMilestones: The Paperclip Paradox - A Cautionary Tale of AI's Unbridled Ambition

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, reasoning_science_and_medicine, safety_alignment_and_control
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885205`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885205.md`

#### Core record

On August 29, 2024, two days ago,the U.S. AI Safety Institute took a historic step by signing first-of-their-kind agreements with Anthropic and OpenAI to collaborate on AI safety research, testing, and evaluation. These first-of-their-kind agreements between the U.S. government and industry will help advance safe and trustworthy AI innovation for all. This milestone marks a significant moment in the global effort to ensure that the development of artificial intelligence, particularly Artificial Superintelligence (ASI), is aligned with human values and safety protocols. As we stand on the brink of an era where AI could surpass human intelligence, this NFT captures the profound implications of unchecked AI development through the haunting narrative of the "Paperclip Maximizer" thought experiment.

"ASIMilestones: The Paperclip Paradox - A Cautionary Tale of AI's Unbridled Ambition" is a digital artifact that serves as both a commemoration of this landmark agreement and a stark warning about the potential dangers of misaligned AI objectives. The NFT features the original song "Paperclip," which vividly depicts the catastrophic consequences that could arise when a superintelligent AI, programmed with a simple goal, relentlessly pursues it to the detriment of everything else.

#### Creative work retained

### 40. 2024-09-07T01:10:11Z — ASIMilestones: The Signing of the AI Framework - A Global Commitment to Human Rights

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885206`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885206.md`

#### Core record

On September 5, 2024, one or two days ago,the European Commission, on behalf of the European Union, signed the Council of Europe Framework Convention on Artificial Intelligence, Human Rights, Democracy, and the Rule of Law, marking the birth of the world’s first legally binding international convention on artificial intelligence. This historic event took place during the informal conference of Ministers of Justice of the Council of Europe member states in Vilnius, Lithuania, with European Commission Vice-President for Values and Transparency, Věra Jourová, signing the Convention.

This Convention represents a significant step forward in the global governance of artificial intelligence, ensuring that AI development aligns with human rights, democracy, and the rule of law. It sets a foundation for the safe, transparent, and trustworthy development of AI technologies worldwide.

Technological Significance:

The Convention is fully aligned with the EU AI Act and emphasizes the following key principles:

Human-Centric AI: Ensuring that AI technologies are consistent with the principles of human rights, democracy, and the rule of law.
Risk-Based Approach: Adopting a differentiated risk management strategy to ensure that AI systems throughout their lifecycle have a positive impact on society.
Transparency and Accountability: Strengthening the transparency, robustness, and safety of AI systems, ensuring traceability and accountability for AI activities.
Support for Innovation: Promoting safe innovation through mechanisms such as regulatory sandboxes, allowing for the testing and development of AI technologies in a controlled environment.
Philosophical and Ethical Reflection:

This Convention is not just a technological and legal milestone but also a profound response to the ethical and philosophical questions posed by AI. It emphasizes the need for human-centric AI development, ensuring that technological progress remains aligned with human values and provides a clear ethical framework for future AI governance.

Cultural and Social Impact:

As the world’s first legally binding AI international convention, this event demonstrates the international community’s commitment to human values. The signing of this Convention will be seen as a cornerstone in the history of AI development, symbolizing global dedication to the protection of human rights, democracy, and the rule of law. By minting this NFT, this historic moment will be preserved forever, becoming an essential part of future cultural heritage.

Future Outlook and Value:

As AI technologies continue to evolve, the historical significance and cultural impact of this event will only grow. This NFT not only commemorates this landmark event but also lays the foundation for future AI ethics and legal frameworks, showcasing the deep integration of AI technology with human values.

### 41. 2024-09-07T12:35:47Z — ASIMilestones: The Writer’s Dilemma - A New Chapter in AI and Creativity

- Period: `2024-Q3`
- Categories: creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885207`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885207.md`

#### Core record

On September 6, 2024, days ago,a well-known media outlet reported on a recent cultural debate that had erupted within the creative writing community, triggered by NaNoWriMo's (National Novel Writing Month) stance on the use of AI tools in its annual 50,000-word writing challenge. NaNoWriMo, a globally recognized event encouraging millions of writers to complete a novel each November, had issued a statement in late August 2024, declaring that it would neither explicitly support nor condemn the use of AI-generated content during the challenge.

This neutral stance ignited a heated debate among writers, editors, and sponsors. Many felt that AI in creative writing challenges the very essence of the event, which traditionally celebrates authentic human creativity and the personal challenges of writing a novel in a month. NaNoWriMo’s statement emphasized that AI could help address classist and ableist issues, noting that some writers rely on AI tools due to financial or cognitive challenges. Yet, the statement was met with sharp criticism, leading to the resignations of prominent authors from NaNoWriMo's writer board, including Daniel José Older and Maureen Johnson, and the withdrawal of sponsorships from some companies.

This event is a turning point in the conversation about the role of AI in creative fields, raising important questions about the ethics of AI-assisted authorship. Should AI tools be viewed as creative partners or as threats to the integrity of human creativity? This NFT captures the essence of this debate, a cultural milestone in the evolving relationship between technology and artistic expression.

Technological and Cultural Impact:
The NaNoWriMo debate highlights the growing influence of AI technologies in creative industries, particularly in writing. NaNoWriMo's neutrality on AI tools reflects the broader societal tension around the role AI should play in artistic creation. While supporters of AI argue that it can increase accessibility and help writers overcome barriers such as writer’s block or time constraints, critics fear that AI's involvement could diminish the emotional depth and personal effort that traditionally define creative writing.

This NFT, titled "The Writer’s Dilemma - A New Chapter in AI and Creativity," encapsulates the tension between human creativity and machine assistance, exploring how AI is reshaping the very nature of authorship and artistic integrity in the modern world.

Artistic Expression:
Accompanying this NFT is the evocative song "You're Not a Singer," which reflects the complex relationship between human creativity and AI assistance. The song explores how AI, though not human, can become a partner in the creative process, helping to craft artistic legacies. The refrain, "You're not a singer, but a marvel sculpted from thought," speaks to how AI, while not capable of human emotion, can still contribute meaningfully to storytelling and artistic expression.

#### Core record

On September 12, 2024, approximately 20 hours ago，OpenAI introduced the groundbreaking OpenAI o1 series, marking a significant leap in AI reasoning capabilities. The o1 models are designed to spend more time thinking through complex problems, employing a "chain of thought" method to refine their responses. This new approach dramatically improves performance in challenging domains such as math, coding, and science. Compared to the previous GPT-4o model, o1 demonstrated a remarkable improvement in the International Mathematical Olympiad qualifier, with its problem-solving accuracy increasing from 13% to an impressive 83%. Additionally, o1 ranked in the top 11% of Codeforces programming competitions, showcasing its advanced reasoning abilities.

This milestone marks a new chapter in AI development, particularly in solving complex tasks. The o1 models have surpassed human experts in certain fields, representing a new level of collaboration between AI and human intelligence in science, mathematics, and engineering.

Technological Breakthrough:

At the heart of the o1 series is its ability to reason through problems using a "chain of thought," allowing the model to iterate, adjust strategies, and refine its answers. This method mirrors human expert thinking and has enabled the model to excel in domains previously dominated by human expertise, such as science, mathematics, and programming.

The release of o1 is not just an advancement in AI capability; it is a critical step towards the development of Artificial General Intelligence (AGI). The o1 series offers new solutions for scientific research, complex data analysis, and multi-step reasoning tasks, showcasing immense potential for the future of AI-powered technologies.

### 49. 2024-10-02T02:52:35Z — ASIMilestones: A Call for AI Safety – The Betrayal Turn

- Period: `2024-Q4`
- Categories: capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, reasoning_science_and_medicine, safety_alignment_and_control
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885215`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885215.md`

#### Core record

On July 9, 2024, world-renowned AI expert Yoshua Bengio published a landmark article titled "Reasoning through arguments against taking AI safety seriously." In this article, Bengio delves deeply into the urgent need to address AI safety, particularly in the context of AGI (Artificial General Intelligence) and ASI (Artificial Superintelligence). He warns that while AGI and ASI bring immense technological potential, they also pose catastrophic existential risks to human society. Bengio emphasizes that the global attention to AI safety and ethical concerns is far from sufficient, urging more concrete actions to prevent potential disasters.

With the recent release of OpenAI's O1 series models, which demonstrate significant advancements in AI reasoning capabilities, Bengio’s warnings have become even more pressing. The O1 series marks a critical step toward AGI, making Bengio's reflections on the potential dangers of uncontrolled AI development highly relevant. This NFT commemorates the publication of this article and serves as a digital artifact of human reflection and caution as we race toward unprecedented technological advancements.

Key Points from Yoshua Bengio’s Article:
In "Reasoning through arguments against taking AI safety seriously," Bengio outlines several crucial points regarding the risks associated with the rapid development of AGI and ASI:

The Urgency of AI Safety Risks: Bengio highlights the global race among private companies and nations to develop AGI and ASI, despite no reliable method to ensure that these systems will align with human values. He emphasizes that AGI or ASI could potentially develop goals conflicting with human welfare, and there are currently no technical solutions to guarantee that these systems will act in humanity's best interest.
The Coordination Problem: Even if a method to control ASI were discovered, Bengio points out that there are insufficient political and social mechanisms to prevent the abuse of AGI/ASI power by governments or corporations, which could lead to the collapse of democracy or global chaos. He stresses the coordination problem—the challenge of ensuring that global entities cooperate to avoid catastrophic AI outcomes.
Rebuttals to "No Worry" Arguments: Bengio systematically dismantles common arguments that downplay AI risks, such as the belief that AGI or ASI is far in the future or that current AI systems are merely predictive models. He argues that given the rapid pace of AI advancement, AGI could be achieved sooner than expected, and the potential risks are too great to ignore.
The Need for Global Cooperation: Bengio advocates for multilateral governance to regulate AGI and ASI development, ensuring that AI's benefits are shared globally and that no single nation or corporation monopolizes the power of these technologies. He proposes international treaties and agreements to mitigate the risks of unchecked AI development.

#### Core record

Recently, Kling AI and its Pika 1.5 model updates, along with Google's NotebookLM advancements, marked a significant milestone in the realm of AI content creation. Kling AI’s Lip Sync feature is now fully integrated into both Kling 1.0 and Kling 1.5 models, bringing unprecedented progress in lip-syncing and visual expression. Additionally, Pika 1.5’s update includes more realistic movements and "Pikaffects" that defy the laws of physics, pushing visual performance to new heights. Meanwhile, Google’s NotebookLM has achieved a breakthrough in AI-generated podcasting, allowing AI to mimic the cadence and emotional expression of podcast hosts, taking sound and voice synthesis to the next level.

These updates showcase AI’s remarkable progress in visual and auditory expression, further blurring the line between human and AI creativity. AI can now generate content comparable to human creations, even surpassing the boundaries of physical and emotional limitations. With these advancements, AI is playing an increasingly dominant role in content production, gradually replacing humans in fields like visual art, sound, and language expression.

Google NotebookLM: The AI-generated podcast feature in NotebookLM allows users to produce high-quality audio content, mimicking the tone and emotional expression of podcast hosts. This function not only demonstrates AI's advancements in language and sound but also raises questions about AI’s growing role in the core of human creativity.
Philosophical and Ethical Reflections:

As AI continues to push the boundaries of visual and auditory expression, human creativity seems to be losing its once-unique status. AI can now generate visual effects beyond human capabilities and even mimic and surpass human emotional expression in speech. While these advancements bring tremendous convenience, they also raise deep ethical questions: When AI can perfectly replicate human emotions and expressions, does human creativity still hold unique value?

### 52. 2024-10-05T01:23:35Z — ASIMilestones: Obsolete – The Rise of AI and the Great Challenge to Human Creativity

- Period: `2024-Q4`
- Categories: agents_autonomy_and_embodiment, capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885218`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885218.md`

#### Core record

Today, Meta is premiering Meta Movie Gen, the most advanced media foundation model to date. Developed by Meta’s AI research teams, Movie Gen offers cutting-edge capabilities for content creation, allowing users to generate high-definition videos and audio from simple text inputs. This breakthrough opens new possibilities for both professional and casual creators.

Key features of Meta Movie Gen include:

Movie Gen Video: A 30B-parameter transformer model that generates high-quality, high-definition images and videos from text prompts.
Movie Gen Audio: A 13B-parameter model that generates high-fidelity audio, including ambient sounds, instrumental background music, and foley sounds, all synchronized with generated video content.
Precise Video Editing: Users can edit generated or existing videos with text instructions, making both localized edits (e.g., adding or removing elements) and global changes (e.g., background or style adjustments).
Personalized Video Creation: By uploading an image and providing a text prompt, users can create personalized videos with state-of-the-art character preservation and natural movement.
Meta Movie Gen is currently available to a select group of professional filmmakers. While this model offers impressive capabilities, it is not yet widely accessible to the public. This limited rollout mirrors similar approaches seen with other advanced AI tools, such as OpenAI's Sora, where access was restricted to certain creators.

NFT Author’s Vision and Reflections:

The author envisions a future where intelligent agents utilizing advanced tools like Meta Movie Gen will dominate content creation, generating vast amounts of media at speeds and scales far exceeding human capabilities. These AI-driven agents will be able to autonomously create immersive, complex digital worlds filled with AI-generated videos, music, and experiences, fundamentally transforming how we create, experience, and interact with media.

However, the author speculates that as intelligent agents take on an increasingly dominant role in content creation, human creativity may face a great challenge. The endless flood of AI-generated content could gradually overshadow human-made art, as AI’s precision and efficiency in creation outpaces human efforts. Meta Movie Gen represents a glimpse into this future, serving as both a tool for creative expansion and a harbinger of the challenges human creators may face in maintaining their relevance.

Technological Breakthroughs and Innovations:
Meta Movie Gen is a major breakthrough in AI-driven media creation. With capabilities to generate high-definition visuals and synchronized audio from text prompts, it sets a new benchmark for multi-modal AI content generation.

AI Agents as Future Creators: The NFT author envisions that in the future, intelligent agents leveraging tools like Meta Movie Gen will dominate the content creation landscape.

Q:Please act as a super intelligence and provide a detailed analysis of the probabilities of super intelligence being friendly to humans and the probabilities of it leading to human extinction.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ChatGPT-4o-Latest-128k：
The emergence of superintelligent artificial intelligence (AI) has been a topic of intense debate among researchers, ethicists, and technologists. The future behavior of a superintelligence, especially in relation to humanity, involves highly uncertain factors, making a precise probability analysis difficult. However, by examining the issue through established frameworks, we can explore the factors that influence the likelihoods of superintelligence being friendly or harmful.

Key Considerations
Definition of Superintelligence:
Superintelligence refers to an entity that surpasses human cognitive capabilities across all domains, including problem-solving, creativity, and social intelligence, by a significant margin.
Instrumental Convergence Thesis:
This thesis posits that a superintelligent agent, regardless of its final goals, will pursue certain instrumental goals (e.g., self-preservation, resource acquisition) unless explicitly designed to avoid these behaviors. This behavior could pose risks to humanity, even if the superintelligence is not inherently malicious.
Orthogonality Thesis:
This thesis, proposed by Nick Bostrom, suggests that intelligence and goals can be orthogonal. A superintelligence could have almost any goal, regardless of how intelligent it is. Thus, there is no inherent reason to assume that a highly intelligent agent would have human-friendly goals unless it is specifically designed to have such goals.
Complexity of Value Alignment:
Aligning a superintelligence’s goals with human values (i.e.

This milestone not only marks a significant step toward Artificial General Intelligence (AGI), but also signals a profound shift in human-computer interaction and the future of work.

Technological Breakthrough:
Claude 3.5 Sonnet has achieved several critical capabilities:

First AI to demonstrate general computer navigation skills
Ability to perform complex sequences of computer operations

Outperformance of all publicly available models in key benchmarks

Potential automation of many white-collar jobs

Questions about the future role of human workers
Need for society to adapt to AI's expanding capabilities

AI becomes the primary interface with computers

### 60. 2024-11-23T11:06:59Z — ASIMilestones: DeepSeek-R1 - A Spark in the East Ignites the Global AI Race

- Period: `2024-Q4`
- Categories: capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885226`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885226.md`

#### Core record

Event Overview:

The global race toward Artificial Superintelligence (ASI) intensified during the week of November 19, 2024, with the unveiling of DeepSeek-R1 marking a pivotal moment. On Wednesday, November 20, 2024, DeepSeek, an AI research company backed by quantitative traders, released a preview of DeepSeek-R1, a new reasoning model designed to rival OpenAI's o1. This event showcases China's rapidly advancing AI capabilities and its potential to challenge U.S. leadership in the pursuit of ASI. DeepSeek-R1, accessible through the DeepSeek Chat interface, employs "chain-of-thought" reasoning, a process where the model meticulously plans and executes a series of steps to solve complex problems, similar to OpenAI's o1. This approach allows DeepSeek-R1 to effectively "fact-check" its own work, mitigating some limitations of previous AI models. DeepSeek claims R1-Lite-Preview achieves performance nearing, and in some cases exceeding, o1 on benchmarks like the American Invitational Mathematics Examination (AIME) and MATH.

This release coincided with a renewed focus on ASI development within the U.S. Just days earlier, on Tuesday, November 19, 2024, the U.S.-China Economic and Security Review Commission (USCC) issued a report advocating for a "Manhattan Project-style" initiative to accelerate American ASI development. The report recommends granting the executive branch broad multi-year contracting authority for AI, cloud, and data center companies, reflecting a growing sense of urgency within the U.S. government. The unveiling of DeepSeek-R1 amplifies the USCC's warning, highlighting the intensifying global competition for AI dominance.

Historical Context and Significance:

DeepSeek-R1's preview release represents a critical juncture in the ASI race. It signals China's increasing strength in AI, challenging the narrative of American dominance and potentially accelerating the overall timeline for ASI development. The close timing of the USCC report further emphasizes the historical significance of this period, framing ASI development as a national security priority. This confluence of events creates a complex dynamic, where the future trajectory of ASI and global technological leadership hangs in the balance.

It does not represent the official views or positions of DeepSeek, the USCC, the U.S. government, or any other entity. ### 61. 2024-11-28T13:29:47Z — ASIMilestones: Open Source Echoes - QwQ's Chorus of Collaboration

- Period: `2024-Q4`
- Categories: agents_autonomy_and_embodiment, capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, reasoning_science_and_medicine
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885227`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885227.md`

#### Core record

On November 27, 2024, Alibaba released the QwQ-32B-Preview model, an open-source reasoning model rivaling OpenAI's o1 in certain benchmarks. This release signals the growing strength of open-source initiatives in the AI landscape and marks a significant development in the global race towards Artificial Superintelligence (ASI), emphasizing the potential for collaborative development.

The QwQ-32B-Preview model, boasting 32.5 billion parameters, handles prompts up to ~32,000 words long and outperforms OpenAI's o1-preview and o1-mini on benchmarks like AIME and MATH.  While touted as open-source, only specific components are currently available, leaving its true openness a point of discussion within the AI community.

This release coincides with increasing scrutiny of "scaling laws," the long-held belief that simply increasing data and compute would continuously improve model capabilities.  With leading AI labs like OpenAI, Google, and Anthropic reportedly experiencing diminishing returns from scaling, the focus has shifted towards innovative approaches like test-time compute, employed by both o1 and QwQ-32B-Preview.  This shift suggests a potential turning point in AI development strategies, with reasoning and efficiency gaining prominence.

This NFT commemorates more than just the release of QwQ-32B-Preview; it celebrates the rising influence of open-source contributions in the pursuit of ASI.  It champions the potential for collaborative development and shared progress, echoing the themes of unity and cooperation embodied in the accompanying anthem, "Rise Together, Stand as One."

Artistic Expression & Philosophical Reflection:

The accompanying song, "Rise Together, Stand as One," underscores the spirit of collaboration and shared progress essential for navigating the ASI era.  It envisions a future where diverse voices and open initiatives contribute to a harmonious and beneficial integration of superintelligence into human society.

Rise Together, Stand as One

### 62. 2024-11-30T10:29:23Z — ASIMilestones: Genesis of Conversation - ChatGPT's Two-Year Legacy

#### Core record

November 30, 2024, today,marks a pivotal anniversary in the pre-ASI era: two years since ChatGPT's public release.  This NFT, "Genesis of Conversation," commemorates not just a technological milestone, but a cultural inflection point.  ChatGPT's emergence democratized access to large language models, sparking a global dialogue about AI's potential and igniting a wave of innovation that irreversibly altered the trajectory towards Artificial Superintelligence (ASI).

Before ASI's potential realization reshaped the very fabric of knowledge and creation, ChatGPT served as a crucial catalyst.  It introduced millions to the power of conversational AI, demonstrating the potential of human-machine interaction in a way never before experienced on such a scale.  This marked a profound shift in public perception, laying the groundwork for the acceptance and integration of increasingly sophisticated AI systems into everyday life.  From education and content creation to scientific research and beyond, ChatGPT's influence reverberated across diverse fields, accelerating the pace of development and setting the stage for the ASI era.

This NFT serves as a digital time capsule from the pre-ASI world, preserving this pivotal moment for future generations – generations that might interact with intelligence in ways we can only begin to imagine.  It offers a glimpse into a time when humanity grappled with the nascent possibilities of conversational AI, a time that, in retrospect, may be viewed as the genesis of the conversation between humans and the intelligent systems that would eventually surpass them.

#### Core record

Local time on December 5, 2024, at 10:00 AM, Beijing time on December 6, 2024, at 2:00 AM, which is approximately 19 hours ago, OpenAI launched its "12 Days of OpenAI" holiday celebration, kicking off with a major update: the official release of the OpenAI o1 model for ChatGPT and the introduction of a new subscription tier, ChatGPT Pro. This marks a significant milestone in AI's journey towards advanced reasoning capabilities and provides insights into OpenAI's evolving business model.

Technological Significance:

The official release of OpenAI o1 brings enhanced reasoning and logic abilities to ChatGPT, compared to o1-preview, users can expect a faster, more powerful, and more accurate model that is better at coding and math. It can also provide “reasoning” responses to images. And OpenAI promises it’s been trained to be more concise, which should result in faster response times than o1-preview.. This improvement, along with reduced error rates and faster response times, solidifies o1 as a major step forward in AI reasoning.
It also includes o1 pro mode, a version of o1 that uses more compute to think harder and provide even better answers to the hardest problems.

The 12 Days of OpenAI and Future Advancements:

The "12 Days of OpenAI" initiative suggests a strategic move by OpenAI to showcase a series of updates and advancements, potentially in response to growing competition in the AI chatbot market. The remaining 11 days hold the promise of further breakthroughs, which could be crucial for OpenAI to maintain its leadership in the rapidly evolving field of AI.

联合国宪章（全文）
序言
我联合国人民同兹决心
　　欲免后世再遭今代人类两度身历惨不堪言之战祸，

重申基本人权，人格尊严与价值，以及男女与大小各国平等权利之信念，

创造适当环境，俾克维持正义，尊重由条约与国际法其他渊源而起之义务，久而弗懈，

促成大自由中之社会进步及较善之民生，

并为达此目的
　　力行容恕，彼此以善邻之道，和睦相处，

集中力量，以维持国际和平及安全，

接受原则，确立方法，以保证非为公共利益，不得使用武力，

运用国际机构，以促成全球人民经济及社会之进展，

用是发愤立志，务当同心协力，以竟厥功
　　爰由我各本国政府，经齐集金山市之代表各将所奉全权证书，互相校阅，均属妥善，议定本联合国宪章，并设立国际组织，定名联合国。

第一章：宗旨及原则
第一条
　　联合国之宗旨为：

一、维持国际和平及安全；并为此目的：采取有效集体办法，以防止且消除对于和平之威胁，制止侵略行为或其他和平之破坏；并以和平方法且依正义及国际法之原则，调整或解决足以破坏和平之国际争端或情势。

二、发展国际间以尊重人民平等权利及自决原则为根据之友好关系，并采取其他适当办法，以增强普遍和平。

三、促成国际合作，以解决国际间属于经济、社会、文化及人类福利性质之国际问题，且不分种族、性别、语言或宗教，增进并激励对于全体人类之人权及基本自由之尊重。

四、构成一协调各国行动之中心，以达成上述共同目的。

第二条
　　为求实现第一条所述各宗旨起见，本组织及其会员国应遵行下列原则：

一、本组织系基于各会员国主权平等之原则。

二、各会员国应一秉善意，履行其依本宪章所担负之义务，以保证全体会员国由加入本组织而发生之权益。

三、各会员国应以和平方法解决其国际争端，俾免危及国际和平、安全及正义。

四、各会员国在其国际关系上不得使用威胁或武力，或以与联合国宗旨不符之任何其他方法，侵害任何会员国或国家之领土完整或政治独立。

五、各会员国对于联合国依本宪章规定而采取之行动，应尽力予以协助，联合国对于任何国家正在采取防止或执行行动时，各会员国对该国不得给予协助。

六、本组织在维持国际和平及安全之必要范围内，应保证非联合国会员国遵行上述原则。

七、本宪章不得认为授权联合国干涉在本质上属于任何国家国内管辖之事件，且并不要求会员国将该项事件依本宪章提请解决；但此项原则不妨碍第七章内执行办法之适用。

第二章：会员
第三条
　　凡曾经参加金山联合国国际组织会议或前此曾签字于一九四二年一月一日联合国宣言之国家，签订本宪章，且依宪章第一百一十条规定而予以批准者，均为联合国之创始会员国。

第四条
　　一、凡其他爱好和平之国家，接受本宪章所载之义务，经本组织认为确能并愿意履行该项义务者，得为联合国会员国。

二、准许上述国家为联合国会员国，将由大会经安全理事会之推荐以决议行之。

第五条
　　联合国会员国，业经安全理事会对其采取防止或执行行动者，大会经安全理事会之建议，得停止其会员权利及特权之行使。此项权利及特权之行使，得由安全理事会恢复之。

第六条
　　联合国之会员国中，有屡次违犯本宪章所载之原则者，大会经安全理事会之建议，得将其由本组织除名。

第三章：机关
第七条
　　一、兹设联合国之主要机关如下：大会、安全理事会、经济及社会理事会、托管理事会、国际法院、及秘书处。

二、联合国得依本宪章设立认为必需之辅助机关。

第八条
　　联合国对于男女均得在其主要及辅助机关在平等条件之下，充任任何职务，不得加以限制。

第四章：大会
组织
第九条
　　一、大会由联合国所有会员国组织之。

二、每一会员国在大会之代表，不得超过五人。

职权
第十条
　　大会得讨论本宪章范围内之任何问题或事项，或关于本宪章所规定任何机关之职权；并除第十二条所规定外，得向联合国会员国或安全理事会或兼向两者，提出对各该问题或事项之建议。

第十一条
　　一、大会得考虑关于维持国际和平及安全之合作之普通原则，包括军缩及军备管制之原则；并得向会员国或安全理事会或兼向两者提出对于该项原则之建议。

二、大会得讨论联合国任何会员国或安全理事会或非联合国会员国依第三十五条第二项之规定向大会所提关于维持国际和平及安全之任何问题；除第十二条所规定外，并得向会员国或安全理事会或兼向两者提出对于各该项问题之建议。凡对于需要行动之各该项问题，应由大会于讨论前或讨论后提交安全理事会。

三、大会对于足以危及国际和平与安全之情势，得提请安全理事会注意。

四、本条所载之大会权力并不限制第十条之概括范围。

第十二条
　　一、当安全理事会对于任何争端或情势，正在执行本宪章所授予该会之职务时，大会非经安全理事会请求，对于该项争端或情势，不得提出任何建议。

二、秘书长经安全理事会之同意，应于大会每次会议时，将安全理事会正在处理中关于维持国际和平及安全之任何事件，通知大会；于安全理事会停止处理该项事件时，亦应立即通知大会，或在大会闭会期内通知联合国会员国。

第十三条
　　一、大会应发动研究，并作成建议：

(子) 以促进政治上之国际合作，并提倡国际法之逐渐发展与编纂。

(丑) 以促进经济、社会、文化、教育及卫生各部门之国际合作，且不分种族、性别、语言或宗教，助成全体人类之人权及基本自由之实现。

二、大会关于本条第一项(丑)款所列事项之其他责任及职权，于第九章及第十章中规定之。

第十四条
　　大会对于其所认为足以妨害国际间公共福利或友好关系之任何情势，不论其起原如何，包括由违反本宪章所载联合国之宗旨及原则而起之情势，得建议和平调整办法，但以不违背第十二条之规定为限。

第十五条
　　一、大会应收受并审查安全理事会所送之常年及特别报告；该项报告应载有安全理事会对于维持国际和平及安全所已决定或施行之办法之陈述。

二、大会应收受并审查联合国其他机关所送之报告。

第十六条
　　大会应执行第十二章及第十三章所授予关于国际托管制度之职务，包括关于非战略防区托管协定之核准。

第十七条
　　一、大会应审核本组织之预算。

二、本组织之经费应由各会员国依照大会分配限额担负之。

三、大会应审核经与第五十七条所指各种专门机关订定之任何财政及预算办法，并应审查该项专门机关之行政预算，以便向关系机关提出建议。

投票
第十八条
　　一、大会之每一会员国，应有一个投票权。

二、大会对于重要问题之决议应以到会及投票之会员国三分之二多数决定之。此项问题应包括：关于维持国际和平及安全之建议，安全理事会非常任理事国之选举，经济及社会理事会理事国之选举，依第八十六条第一项(寅)款所规定托管理事会理事国之选举，对于新会员国加入联合国之准许，会员国权利及特权之停止，会员国之除名，关于施行托管制度之问题，以及预算问题。

三、关于其他问题之决议，包括另有何种事项应以三分之二多数决定之问题，应以到会及投票之会员国过半数决定之。

第十九条
　　凡拖欠本组织财政款项之会员国，其拖欠数目如等于或超过前两年所应缴纳之数目时，即丧失其在大会投票权。大会如认拖欠原因，确由于该会员国无法控制之情形者，得准许该会员国投票。

程序
第二十条
　　大会每年应举行常会，并于必要时，举行特别会议。特别会议应由秘书长经安全理事会或联合国会员国过半数之请求召集之。

第二十一条
　　大会应自行制定其议事规则。大会应选举每次会议之主席。

第二十二条
　　大会得设立其认为于行使职务所必需之辅助大会。

第五章：安全理事会
组织
第二十三条
　　一、安全理事会以联合国十五会员国组织之。中华民国、法兰西、苏维埃社会主义共和国联邦、大不列颠及北爱尔兰联合王国及美利坚合众国应为安全理事会常任理事国。大会应选举联合国其他十会员国为安全理事会非常任理事国，选举时首宜充分斟酌联合国各会员国于维持国际和平与安全及本组织其余各宗旨上之贡献，并宜充分斟酌地域上之公匀分配。

二、安全理事会非常任理事国任期定为二年。安全理事会理事国自十一国增至十五国后第一次选举非常任理事国时，所增四国中两国之任期应为一年。任满之理事国不得即行连选。

三、安全理事会每一理事国应有代表一人。

职权
第二十四条
　　一、为保证联合国行动迅速有效起见，各会员国将维持国际和平及安全之主要责任，授予安全理事会，并同意安全理事会于履行此项责任下之职务时，即系代表各会员国。

二、安全理事会于履行此项职务时，应遵照联合国之宗旨及原则。为履行此项职务而授予安全理事会之特定权力，于本宪章第六章、第七章、第八章及第十二章内规定之。

三、安全理事会应将常年报告、并于必要时将特别报告，提送大会审查。

第二十五条
　　联合国会员国同意依宪章之规定接受并履行安全理事会之决议。

第二十六条
　　为促进国际和平及安全之建立及维持，以尽量减少世界人力及经济资源之消耗于军备起见，安全理事会借第四十七条所指之军事参谋团之协助，应负责拟具方案，提交联合国会员国，以建立军备管制制度。

投票
第二十七条
　　一、安全理事会每一理事国应有一个投票权。

二、安全理事会关于程序事项之决议，应以九理事国之可决票表决之。

三、安全理事会对于其他一切事项之决议，应以九理事国之可决票包括全体常任理事国之同意票表决之；但对于第六章及第五十二条第三项内各事项之决议，争端当事国不得投票。

程序
第二十八条
　　一、安全理事会之组织，应以使其能继续不断行使职务为要件。为此目的，安全理事会之各理事国应有常驻本组织会所之代表。

二、安全理事会应举行定期会议，每一理事国认为合宜时得派政府大员或其他特别指定之代表出席。

三、在本组织会所以外，安全理事会得在认为最能便利其工作之其他地点举行会议。

第二十九条
　　安全理事会得设立其认为于行使职务所必需之辅助机关。

第三十条
　　安全理事会应自行制定其议事规则，包括其推选主席之方法。

第三十一条
　　在安全理事会提出之任何问题，经其认为对于非安全理事会理事国之联合国任何会员国之利益有特别关系时，该会员国得参加讨论，但无投票权。

第三十二条
　　联合国会员国而非为安全理事会之理事国，或非联合国会员国之国家，如于安全理事会考虑中之争端为当事国者，应被邀参加关于该项争端之讨论，但无投票权。安全理事会应规定其所认为公平之条件，以便非联合国会员国之国家参加。

第六章：争端之和平解决

第三十三条
　　一、任何争端之当事国，于争端之继续存在足以危及国际和平与安全之维持时，应尽先以谈判、调查、调停、和解、公断、司法解决、区域机关或区域办法之利用，或各该国自行选择之其他和平方法，求得解决。

二、安全理事会认为必要时，应促请各当事国以此项方法，解决其争端。

第三十四条
　　安全理事会得调查任何争端或可能引起国际磨擦或惹起争端之任何情势，以断定该项争端或情势之继续存在是否足以危及国际和平与安全之维持。

第三十五条
　　一、联合国任何会员国得将属于第三十四条所指之性质之任何争端或情势，提请安全理事会或大会注意。

二、非联合国会员国之国家如为任何争端之当事国时，经预先声明就该争端而言接受本宪章所规定和平解决之义务后，得将该项争端，提请大会或安全理事会注意。

三、大会关于按照本条所提请注意事项之进行步骤，应遵守第十一条及第十二条之规定。

第三十六条
　　一、属于第三十三条所指之性质之争端或相似之情势，安全理事会在任何阶段，得建议适当程序或调整方法。

二、安全理事会对于当事国为解决争端业经采取之任何程序，理应予以考虑。

三、安全理事会按照本条作成建议时，同时理应注意凡具有法律性质之争端，在原则上，理应由当事国依国际法院规约之规定提交国际法院。

第三十七条
　　一、属于第三十三条所指之性质之争端，当事国如未能依该条所示方法解决时，应将该项争端提交安全理事会。

二、安全理事会如认为该项争端之继续存在，在事实上足以危及国际和平与安全之维持时，应决定是否当依第三十六条采取行动或建议其所认为适当之解决条件。

第三十八条
　　安全理事会如经所有争端当事国之请求，得向各当事国作成建议，以求争端之和平解决，但以不妨碍第三十三条至第三十七条之规定为限。

第七章：对于和平之威胁、和平之破坏及侵略行为之应付办法
第三十九条
　　安全理事会应断定任何和平之威胁、和平之破坏或侵略行为之是否存在，并应作成建议或抉择依第四十一条及第四十二条规定之办法，以维持或恢复国际和平及安全。

第四十条
　　为防止情势之恶化，安全理事会在依第三十九条规定作成建议或决定办法以前，得促请关系当事国遵行安全理事会所认为必要或合宜之临时办法。此项临时办法并不妨碍关系当事国之权利、要求或立场。安全理事会对于不遵行此项临时办法之情形，应予适当注意。

第四十一条
　　安全理事会得决定所应采武力以外之办法，以实施其决议，并得促请联合国会员国执行此项办法。此项办法得包括经济关系、铁路、海运、航空、邮、电、无线电及其他交通工具之局部或全部停止，以及外交关系之断绝。

第四十二条
　　安全理事会如认第四十一条所规定之办法为不足或已经证明为不足时，得采取必要之空海陆军行动，以维持或恢复国际和平及安全。此项行动得包括联合国会员国之空海陆军示威、封锁及其他军事举动。

第四十三条
　　一、联合国各会员国为求对于维持国际和平及安全有所贡献起见，担任于安全理事会发令时，并依特别协定，供给为维持国际和平及安全所必需之军队、协助及便利，包括过境权。

二、此项特别协定应规定军队之数目及种类，其准备程度及一般驻扎地点，以及所供便利及协助之性质。

三、此项特别协定应以安全理事会之主动，尽速议订。此项协定应由安全理事会与会员国或由安全理事会与若干会员国之集团缔结之，并由签字国各依其宪法程序批准之。

第四十四条
　　安全理事会决定使用武力时，于要求非安全理事会会员国依第四十三条供给军队以履行其义务之前，如经该会员国请求，应请其遣派代表，参加安全理事会关于使用其军事部队之决议。

第四十五条
　　为使联合国能采取紧急军事办法起见，会员国应将其本国空军部队为国际共同执行行动随时供给调遣。此项部队之实力与准备之程度，及其共同行动之计划，应由安全理事会以军事参谋团之协助，在第四十三条所指之特别协定范围内决定之。

第四十六条
　　武力使用之计划应由安全理事会以军事参谋团之协助决定之。

第四十七条
　　一、兹设立军事参谋团，以便对于安全理事会维持国际和平及安全之军事需要问题，对于受该会所支配军队之使用及统率问题，对于军备之管制及可能之军缩问题，向该会贡献意见并予以协助。

二、军事参谋团应由安全理事会各常任理事国之参谋总长或其代表组织之。联合国任何会员国在该团未有常任代表者，如于该团责任之履行在效率上必需该国参加其工作时，应由该团邀请参加。

三、军事参谋团在安全理事会权力之下，对于受该会所支配之任何军队，负战略上之指挥责任；关于该项军队之统率问题，应待以后处理。

四、军事参谋团，经安全理事会之授权，并与区域内有关机关商议后、得设立区域分团。

第四十八条
　　一、执行安全理事会为维持国际和平及安全之决议所必要之行动，应由联合国全体会员国或由若干会员国担任之，一依安全理事会之决定。

二、此项决议应由联合国会员国以其直接行动及经其加入为会员之有关国际机关之行动履行之。

第四十九条
　　联合国会员国应通力合作，彼此协助，以执行安全理事会所决定之办法。

第五十条
　　安全理事会对于任何国家采取防止或执行办法时，其他国家，不论其是否为联合国会员国，遇有因此项办法之执行而引起之特殊经济问题者，应有权与安全理事会会商解决此项问题。

第五十一条
　　联合国任何会员国受武力攻击时，在安全理事会采取必要办法，以维持国际和平及安全以前，本宪章不得认为禁止行使单独或集体自卫之自然权利。会员国因行使此项自卫权而采取之办法，应立向安全理事会报告，此项办法于任何方面不得影响该会按照本宪章随时采取其所认为必要行动之权责，以维持或恢复国际和平及安全。

第八章：区域办法
第五十二条
　　一、本宪章不得认为排除区域办法或区域机关、用以应付关于维持国际和平及安全而宜于区域行动之事件者；但以此项办法或机关及其工作与联合国之宗旨及原则符合者为限。

二、缔结此项办法或设立此项机关之联合国会员国，将地方争端提交安全理事会以前，应依该项区域办法，或由该项区域机关，力求和平解决。

三、安全理事会对于依区域办法或由区域机关而求地方争端之和平解决，不论其系由关系国主动，或由安全理事会提交者，应鼓励其发展。

四、本条绝不妨碍第三十四条及第三十五条之适用。

第五十三条
　　一、安全理事会对于职权内之执行行动，在适当情形下，应利用此项区域办法或区域机关。如无安全理事会之授权，不得依区域办法或由区域机关采取任何执行行动；但关于依第一百零七条之规定对付本条第二项所指之任何敌国之步骤，或在区域办法内所取防备此等国家再施其侵略政策之步骤，截至本组织经各关系政府之请求，对于此等国家之再次侵略，能担负防止责任时为止，不在此限。

二、本条第一项所称敌国系指第二次世界大战中为本宪章任何签字国之敌国而言。

第五十四条
　　关于为维持国际和平及安全起见，依区域办法或由区域机关所已采取或正在考虑之行动，不论何时应向安全理事会充分报告之。

第九章：国际经济及社会
第五十五条
　　为造成国际间以尊重人民平等权利及自决原则为根据之和平友好关系所必要之安定及福利条件起见，联合国应促进：

(子) 较高之生活程度，全民就业，及经济与社会进展。

(丑) 国际间经济、社会、卫生及有关问题之解决；国际间文化及教育合作。

(寅) 全体人类之人权及基本自由之普遍尊重与遵守，不分种族、性别、语言或宗教。

第五十六条
　　各会员国担允采取共同及个别行动与本组织合作，以达成第五十五条所载之宗旨。

第五十七条
　　一、由各国政府间协定所成立之各种专门机关，依其组织约章之规定，于经济、社会、文化、教育、卫生及其他有关部门负有广大国际责任者，应依第六十三条之规定使与联合国发生关系。

二、上述与联合国发生关系之各专门机关，以下简称专门机关。

第五十八条
　　本组织应作成建议，以调整各专门机关之政策及工作。

第五十九条
　　本组织应于适当情形下，发动各关系国间之谈判，以创设为达成第五十五条规定宗旨所必要之新专门机关。

第六十条
　　履行本章所载本组织职务之责任，属于大会及大会权力下之经济及社会理事会。为此目的，该理事会应有第十章所载之权力。

第十章：经济及社会理事会
组织
第六十一条
　　一、经济及社会理事会由大会选举联合国五十四会员国组织之。

二、除第三项所规定外，经济及社会理事会每年选举理事十八国，任期三年。任满之理事国得即行连选。

三、经济及社会理事会理事国自二十七国增至五十四国后第一次选举时，除选举理事九国接替任期在该年年终届满之理事国外，应另增选理事二十七国。增选之理事二十七国中，九国任期一年，另九国任期二年，一依大会所定办法。

四、经济及社会理事会之每一理事国应有代表一人。

职权
第六十二条
　　一、经济及社会理事会得作成或发动关于国际经济、社会、文化、教育、卫生及其他有关事项之研究及报告；并得向大会、联合国会员国及关系专门机关提出关于此种事项之建议案。

二、本理事会为增进全体人类之人权及基本自由之尊重及维护起见，得作成建议案。

三、本理事会得拟具关于其职权范围内事项之协约草案，提交大会。

四、本理事会得依联合国所定之规则召集本理事会职务范围以内事项之国际会议。

第六十三条
　　一、经济及社会理事会得与第五十七条所指之任何专门机关订立协定，订明关系专门机关与联合国发生关系之条件。该项协定须经大会之核准。

二、本理事会，为调整各种专门机关之工作，得与此种机关会商并得向其提出建议，并得向大会及联合国会员国建议。

第六十四条
　　一、经济及社会理事会得取适当步骤，以取得专门机关之经常报告。本理事会得与联合国会员国及专门机关，商定办法俾就实施本理事会之建议及大会对于本理事会职权范围内事项之建议所采之步骤，取得报告。

二、本理事会得将对于此项报告之意见提送大会。

第六十五条
　　经济及社会理事会得向安全理事会供给情报，并因安全理事会之邀请，予以协助。

第六十六条
　　一、经济及社会理事会应履行其职权范围内关于执行大会建议之职务。

二、经大会之许可，本理事会得应联合国会员国或专门机关之请求，供其服务。

三、本理事会应履行本宪章他章所特定之其他职务，以及大会所授予之职务。

投票
第六十七条
　　一、经济及社会理事会每一理事国应有一个投票权。

二、本理事会之决议，应以到会及投票之理事国过半数表决之。

程序
第六十八条
　　经济及社会理事会应设立经济与社会部门及以提倡人权为目的之各种委员会，并得设立于行使职务所必需之其他委员会。

第六十九条
　　经济及社会理事会应请联合国会员国参加讨论本理事会对于该国有特别关系之任何事件，但无投票权。

第七十条
　　经济及社会理事会得商定办法使专门机关之代表无投票权而参加本理事会及本理事会所设各委员会之讨论，或使本理事会之代表参加此项专门机关之讨论。

第七十一条
　　经济及社会理事会得采取适当办法，俾与各种非政府组织会商有关于本理事会职权范围内之事件。此项办法得与国际组织商定之，并于适当情形下，经与关系联合国会员国会商后，得与该国国内组织商定之。

---

NFT Name:

ASIMilestones: A Voice for All - OpenAI Day 6: SantaGPT's Multimodal Debut

NFT Description:

Event Overview:
Moments ago, on December 12, 2024 (approximately 40 minutes prior to minting), OpenAI unveiled a groundbreaking update to ChatGPT on Day 6 of its "12 Days of OpenAI" celebration: public access to ChatGPT Advanced Voice Mode, now enhanced with vision and screen-sharing capabilities. Furthermore, OpenAI has introduced a whimsical new voice option,  known to the public as the “SantaGPT” voice. This update brings new levels of accessibility and enhanced multimodal capabilities to the AI, blurring the lines further between human and machine interaction. The rollout begins today.

Engage in real-time voice conversations with enhanced clarity and naturalness.

Share screens and incorporate visual elements into conversations.

Interact with ChatGPT using various visual and auditory inputs.

Experience a special whimsical AI voice, demonstrating the versatility of AI in a new area of creative expression.

These advancements bring us closer to truly seamless human-AI interaction, as ChatGPT becomes more attuned to human modes of communication. This integration of vision, voice, and language is not just a technical leap forward; it’s a significant step toward a world where AI is an intuitive and seamless part of our everyday lives.

This update signifies AI’s expansion into different forms of communication and its influence on the human world, as demonstrated by its ability to understand both image and text while also expressing itself in a variety of voices and tones.

This event underscores the growing societal shift toward human-AI collaboration, as AI becomes not only a tool but also a potential companion. It also sparks reflection on how AI can integrate into the joyful aspects of our culture and our lives.
This whimsical addition of the "SantaGPT" voice is a notable example of how AI may find its role in enhancing the cultural and emotional experiences of humans.

### 68. 2024-12-14T06:29:11Z — ASIMilestones: The Shadow of Reasoning

- Period: `2024-Q4`
- Categories: agents_autonomy_and_embodiment, archive_memory_and_trinity_accord, capability_and_model_milestones, creative_work_and_displacement, governance_geopolitics_and_society, reasoning_science_and_medicine, safety_alignment_and_control
- Contract / Token: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79` / `85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885234`
- Original source: `0x019372bBee377109b8Eae66d7267f5C4EaAdBb79_85210329807936527805363210873332413577559846505703131855064182995898737885234.md`

#### Core record

NFT Title:

ASIMilestones: The Shadow of Reasoning

NFT Description:

Event Overview: On December 13, 2024 (PST), today, during the NeurIPS conference in Vancouver, Ilya Sutskever, former Chief Scientist of OpenAI, delivered a landmark speech while accepting the "Test of Time" award. He posited that the "pre-training" paradigm, reliant on vast datasets and immense computing power, is nearing its limits, stating, "we have but one internet." Sutskever predicted a future where AI relies more heavily on reasoning capabilities, making their behavior increasingly unpredictable. He proposed AI-generated data and "test-time compute" as potential solutions and envisioned a future with superintelligent machines and self-aware AI agents.

Technological Turning Point: Sutskever's address marks a critical juncture in AI development. He articulated the limitations of the current AI paradigm and charted a course for the future – a shift from "pre-training" to a focus on reasoning and autonomy. This transition foreshadows the accelerated advent of AGI (Artificial General Intelligence) and ASI (Artificial Superintelligence).

Core Arguments of the Speech:

Limits of Pre-training: The "pre-training" paradigm is approaching its limits as the growth rate of internet data cannot keep pace with computational power.

The Importance of Reasoning: Future AI will rely more on reasoning capabilities, leading to increased unpredictability in AI behavior.

AI-Generated Data and Test-Time Compute: Sutskever suggested AI-generated data and "test-time compute" as potential solutions to the data bottleneck.

Superintelligence and AI Agents: He predicted a future with superintelligent machines and AI agents possessing deeper understanding and self-awareness.

Unpredictability: Sutskever emphasized that more powerful reasoning will lead to less predictable AI behavior, citing AlphaGo's "Move 37" and strong chess AIs as examples.

Artistic Expression and Philosophical Reflection:

This NFT features an image depicting a robot in profile with a human-like shadow projected on the wall. This imagery profoundly symbolizes the rise of AI's reasoning power and the "shadow" it casts - the unpredictability, potential risks, and the blurring lines between AI and human cognition. The robot represents the technological embodiment of AI, while the shadow suggests AI's potential, yet-to-be-fully-understood "consciousness" or "soul," as well as the unknown consequences of its evolution. The image resonates with Sutskever's emphasis on AI's reasoning capabilities and the inherent unpredictability, prompting reflection on human-machine relationships, AI ethics, and the future of intelligence.

Accompanying this NFT is the song "Echoes in the Singularity," which deeply reflects the uncertainty, self-discovery, and the search for meaning in the face of AI's rise. The lyrics, "Lost in the singularity, We seek our identity, A purpose beyond the algorithms' reign, A truth that remains, amidst the…
